**元智大學 社會暨政策科學學系 必修科目表**

**Department of Social and Policy Sciences, Yuan Ze University**

**List of Required Courses**

**（112學年度入學新生適用）**

**(Applicable to Students Admitted in Academic Year of 2023)**

112.04.19 一一一學年度第六次教務會議通過

112.05.31 一一一學年度第七次教務會議通過

114.12.24 一一四學年度第四次教務會議修訂通過

115.04.29 一一四學年度第七次教務會議修訂通過

<table><tr><td rowspan="2"><p>學年Academic Year</p><p>學期Semester</p><p>科目Subject</p></td><td colspan="5"><p>第一學年1<sup>st</sup> Academic Year</p></td><td colspan="7"><p>第二學年2<sup>nd</sup> Academic Year</p></td><td colspan="6"><p>第三學年3<sup>rd</sup> Academic Year</p></td><td colspan="4"><p>第四學年4<sup>th</sup> Academic Year</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>上Fall</p></td><td colspan="4"><p>下Spring</p></td><td colspan="4"><p>上Fall</p></td><td colspan="3"><p>下Spring</p></td><td colspan="3"><p>上Fall</p></td><td colspan="3"><p>下Spring</p></td><td colspan="3"><p>上Fall</p></td><td><p>下Spring</p></td></tr><tr><td rowspan="5"><p>共同必修科目</p><p>University Compulsory</p><p>（17）</p></td><td><p>國文（一）</p><p>Chinese (I)</p><p>（2）</p></td><td colspan="4"><p>國文（二）</p><p>Chinese (II)</p><p>（2）</p></td><td colspan="4"></td><td colspan="3"></td><td colspan="3"></td><td colspan="3"></td><td colspan="3"></td><td></td></tr><tr><td><p>英語（一）</p><p>English (I)</p><p>（2）</p></td><td colspan="4"><p>英語（二）</p><p>English (II)</p><p>（2）</p></td><td colspan="4"></td><td colspan="3"></td><td colspan="3"></td><td colspan="3"></td><td colspan="3"></td><td></td></tr><tr><td colspan="22"><p>外語課程應修習10學分。</p><ol><li>「英語（一）」及「英語（二）」為基礎課程，採能力分級上課，共計二學期四學分。</li><li>除了「英語（一）」及「英語（二）」外，畢業前應修畢三個不同主題式英語課程，共三學期5學分。</li><li>大一英語能力後測「TOEIC模擬測驗」成績未達350分者，應修習「應試加強班」(EL260)。修習「應試加強班」期間之期末TOEIC模擬測驗成績未達350分者，則該科成績將「不及格」，並應再次修習「應試加強班」，直到取得TOEIC模擬測驗分數達350分(含)始得修習其他主題式英語課程。</li><li>另開設「英語檢定」(EL360)計一學期1學分，「英語檢定」之修課限制與注意事項，請參照「通識外語『英語檢定』修課規定」，並由通識教學部公佈後施行。</li></ol><p>外國學生改修華語須經國際語言文化中心審核通過始可改修華語課程10學分，其華語課程10學分應含「華語檢定」1學分，「華語檢定」修課限制與注意事項，請參照「通識外語『英語檢定』修課規定」。</p><p>凡本校大學部外國學生修習「華語（一）」或「華語（二）」任一課程成績未達60分，不得修習「華語（三）」、「華語（四）」。若修習「華語（三）」、「華語（四）」任一課程成績未達60分，不得修習「華語（五）」或「華語檢定」（EL372）。</p><p>The undergraduate students must complete 10 required credits of foreign language courses.</p><ol><li>English (I) &amp; (II) for the total 4 credits: English (I) and (II) are 4 credit elementary courses for the freshmen who are grouped on English competence; to complete within two semesters.</li><li>English thematic course for the total 5 credits: English thematic courses are 5-credit English courses; students are required to obtain 5 credits through 3 different thematic courses for graduation. </li><li>Students who do not reach the 350-point threshold of TOEIC Mock Exam in the end of the freshman year must take “English Testing” (EL260) course. Students will fail the course if they do not score higher than 350 points in TOEIC Mock Exam by the end of the course, and must repeatedly take the course until they can score higher than 350 points. </li><li>“English Testing” (EL360) for the total 1 credit: For the requirements of registering “English Testing”, please refer to "the Regulation for Registering English Test" announced and implemented by the College of General Education.</li></ol><p>Foreign students need approval by ILCC for taking 10 credits of Mandarin Chinese courses as alternative courses of English.</p><p>The undergraduate foreign students must pass Mandarin Chinese (I) and (II) before taking Mandarin Chinese (III) and (IV). Students must pass Mandarin Chinese (III) and (IV) before taking Mandarin Chinese (V) and Chinese Proficiency Test (EL372).</p><p>英語檢定English Testing（1）、經典選讀A Guide to Classics（2）、服務學習Service Learning（1）</p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="2"><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td colspan="3"><p>興趣選項體育optional physical education（0）</p></td><td colspan="3"><p>興趣選項體育optional physical education（0）</p></td><td colspan="3"></td><td colspan="3"></td><td colspan="3"></td><td colspan="3"></td></tr><tr><td colspan="22"><p>大學部必須修習4學期體育課程；其中2學期為大一體育課程原班級上課，另2學期為興趣選項體育課程。</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>通識教育科目General Education</p><p>（10）</p></td><td colspan="22"><p>The undergraduate students must attend the physical education course for 4 semesters; 2 semesters for the freshman physical education courses, the other two semesters for the optional physical education courses.</p><p>通識課程分為人文藝術、自然科學、社會科學及生命科學四大類。學生須於四大領域中各選修2學分課程，共計8學分。General Education program comprises four categories：Humanities, Natural Science, Social Science and Life Science. Students are required to take a 2-credit course from each category to get 8 credits before graduation.</p><p>通識跨域課程General Education Interdisciplinary Course：此2學分學生可自由於通識講座課程、微課自主學習或在地多元文化課群中選課。惟外籍生與工程學院英語學士班、資訊學院英語學士班、人文社會學院英語學士班、電機通訊學院英語學士班學生仍須於四大領域中選課，依各院修課規定辦理。Students can select the 2 credits from a General Education Lecture course, Micro Credit courses, Self-Study courses, or Local-Multicultural courses. Only foreign students and undergraduates of International Programs in the Colleges of Engineering, Informatics, Humanities and Social Sciences, as well as Electrical and Communication Engineering are required to take a 2-credit course from the four categories according to each college’s policy before graduation.</p><p>通識4大領域各選修2學分共計8學分，其餘2學分之通識跨域課程改為「必選修｣，可於通識講座課程、微課自主學習或在地多元文化課群中選課，亦即不可由四大領域中選課。</p><p>必修社會科學領域:法學緒論2學分。Compulsory Social Sciences Courses: Introduction to Law, 2 Credits</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>院必修科目</p><p>College</p><p>Compulsory</p><p>（4）</p></td><td colspan="22"><p>程式語言共4學分，依各院修課規則辦理。</p><p>The Fundamental Computer Programming has 4 credits in total, which is subject to the rules of each college.</p><p>基礎程式設計（一） Fundamental Computer Programming (I)（2）(課號:HS002)、基礎程式設計（二） Fundamental Computer Programmin (Π)（2）(課號:HS003)</p></td></tr><tr><td rowspan="4"><p>系必修科目Department Compulsory</p><p> (35)</p></td><td colspan="3"><p>SC133</p><p>社會學</p><p>Sociology </p><p>（3）</p></td><td colspan="3"><p>SC219</p><p>社會心理學</p><p>Social Psychology （3）</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>SC203</p><p>社會統計(上)</p><p>Social Statistics (I)（2）</p></td><td colspan="3"><p>SC208</p><p>社會統計(下)</p><p>Social Statistics (II)（2）</p></td><td colspan="22"><ol><li>有關共同必修及通識教育科目之詳細規定，另依據「元智大學共同必修科目表」之規定辦理。</li></ol><p>Please refer to Yuan Ze University Common Required Course List for General Education courses information and regulations.</p><ol><li>通識教育科目學分只採計至多10學分，超修之學分將不列入畢業學分。國際語言中心選修課無法認列本系選修</li></ol><p>The maximum credit number for general education courses is 10. The exceeding credits will not be counted. International Language Center selective courses can not be recognized.</p><ol><li>終端學習課程： 實地工作 （實習）（二）</li></ol><p>The experiential learning courses：Field Practice (II)</p><ol><li>政策規劃與執行課程（課號SC432）為本系必修「議題導向實作專題課程」3學分. </li></ol><p>Policy Planning and implementation (course code SC432) is a compulsory three-credit course of "Topic and Implementation-oriented courses".</p><ol><li>「大數據與政策分析應用基礎」課程（課號SC132）、「大數據與政策分析應用進階」課程（課號SC249）為本系「數位應用相關課程｣，畢業前須通過至少2門「數位應用相關課程」(可至本系或外系修習)。(通識程式語言課程為本校發展「數位跨域」的基礎課程，不重複列為每位學生必須修習的兩門「數位應用相關課程」。資訊概論、計算機概論、網路概論等課程不可列入「數位應用相關課程」，須強調利用數位技術，實作出數位作品。)</li></ol><p>“Big Data and Policy Analysis Application Basic (course code SC132)”, and “Big Data and Policy Analysis Advanced (course code SC249)” are courses of “digital application courses.” Students are required to take and pass at least two “digital application courses.” (Student may take “digital application courses” from another department.)</p><ol><li>本系同學總共必須修滿 128學分方可畢業，包括共同必修及通識課程共27學分、院必修程式語言課程共4學分、本系必修35學分，選修62學分（外系選修至多承認24學分，與他系合作之學程，依學程規定承認最高學分）。</li></ol><p>Student of Department of Social and Policy Sciences are required to accomplished 128 credits in total for graduation, including 27 credits for required common courses and general education courses, 4 credits for college compulsory courses--fundamental computer programming, 35 credits for the departmental compulsory courses, and 62 additional credits for elective courses among which students are allowed to take up to 24 credits of courses from other departments.</p><ol><li>為增進學生英文能力，鼓勵選修英語授課課程(含英專班)，其修習之課程科目及學分數之認抵需依學系規定辦理。</li></ol><p>To improve students’ English, we encourage students to take the courses in English (including English Bachelor), which courses and credits waiver and transference should be standardized by each department.</p><ol><li>自106學年度起軍訓課程由必修改為選修，該學分納入當學期修課學分數計算，但不納入畢業總學分計算。</li></ol><p>The military education courses are no longer compulsory starting the 106 academic year. The military education courses will not be accumulated to the graduation requirements, but they can be counted as taken credits for each semester.</p><ol><li>學生選修課程模組分類：「社會/政府行政」、「社會工作」、「社會企劃」三大軸向，各含有核心與精選次課程模組。學生須選修二核心課程模組與二精選課程模組各三門課。相關選修課程模組分類表請參閱「社會暨政策科學學系選修課程模組」。</li></ol><p>There are three focused, selective course dimensions towards the fields of social/governmental administration, social work, and social planning. Each dimension contains a core course module and a featured course module. Students must take two core modules and three courses each from two featured modules to fulfill graduation requirements.</p><ol><li>學生必須參與演講或活動才能取得職涯發展課程（一）至（六）的成績。前三場系內演講或活動每場計25分，其餘活動（無論系內或系外）每場計10分。</li></ol><p>Students must attend talks or activities to earn grades for The Development of Career (I), (II), (III), (IV), (V), and (VI) courses. Each of the first three department-organized talks or activities is counted as 25 points, while each additional talk or activity (whether within or outside the department) is counted as 10 points."  </p></td></tr></table>

AA-CP-04-CF02 (1.4版)／113.12.16修訂
```

(Course Name: Fundamental Computer Programming(一)、Fundamental Computer Programming(二))</p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="18"><p>外語課程應依「通識外語修課規定」修習，共計10學分。</p><ol><li>「英語（一）」及「英語（二）」為基礎課程，採能力分級上課，共計二學期四學分。</li><li>除了「英語（一）」及「英語（二）」外，應修習主題式英語課程三學期5學分，畢業前需修畢三個不同英語課程，始取得畢業資格。大一英語能力後測TOEIC模擬測驗成績未達350分者，應修習「應試加強班」，修習「應試加強班」期間之期末TOEIC模擬測驗成績未達350分者，則該科成績將「不及格」，並應再次修習「應試加強班」，直到取得TOEIC模擬測驗分數達350分(含)始得修習其他主題式英語課程。</li><li>另開設「英語檢定」計一學期1學分，「英語檢定」之修課限制與注意事項，請參照「英語檢定」修課規定，並由通識教學部公佈後施行。</li></ol><p>外國學生改修華語須經國際語言文化中心審核通過始可改修華語課程10學分，其華語課程10學分應含「華語檢定」1學分，「華語檢定」修課限制與注事意項，請參照「英語檢定」修課規定。</p><p>凡本校大學部外國學生(不含交換生)修習「華語一」或「華語二」任一課程成績未達60分，不得修習「華語三」、「華語四」、「華語五」、「華語六」，若修習「華語三」、「華語四」任一課程成績未達60分，不得修習「華語五」或「華語檢定」。</p><p>The undergraduate students must complete 10 required credits of foreign language courses as follows:</p><ol><li>English (I) &amp; (II) for the total 4 credits: English (I) and (II) are 4 credit elementary courses for the freshmen who are grouped on English competence; to complete within two semesters.</li><li>English thematic course for the total 5 credits: English thematic courses are 5-credit English courses; students are required to obtain 5 credits through 3 different thematic courses for graduation. </li></ol><p>Students who do not reach the 350 points threshold of the English posttest in the end of the freshman year must take “English Testing” course. Students will fail the course if they do not score higher than 350 points in TOEIC simulated test by the end of the course, and must repeatedly take the course until they can score higher than 350 points. </p><ol><li>English Test for the total 1 credit: For the requirements of registering “English Testing”, please refer to "the Regulation for Registering English Test" announced and implemented by the College of General Education</li></ol><p>Foreign students need approval by ILCC for taking 10 credits of Mandarin Chinese courses as alternative courses of English.</p><p>The undergraduate foreign students, exchange students excluded, must score 60 points or higher to pass Mandarin Chinese (I) and (II) before taking Mandarin Chinese (III), (IV), (V), and (VI). Students must score 60 points or higher in Mandarin Chinese (III) and (IV) before taking Mandarin Chinese (V) and (VI).</p><p>英語檢定English Testing（1）、經典五十Fifty Canonized Books（2）、服務學習Service Learning（1）</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td colspan="4"><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td colspan="3"><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td colspan="3"><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td></td><td colspan="2"></td><td colspan="2"></td><td colspan="2"></td></tr><tr><td colspan="18"><p>體育除修習大一至大二4個學期外，另需通過「游泳能力檢定」及「心肺適能檢定」等二項檢測，列為畢業門檻。</p><p>Beside taking PE courses for 4 semesters (Year 1 to 2), students must pass both swimming and cardiopulmonary function tests.</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>通識教育科目General Education</p><p>（10）</p></td><td colspan="18"><p>通識課程分為人文藝術、自然科學、社會科學及生命科學四大類。學生須於四大領域中各選修2學分課程，共計8學分。General Education program comprises four categories：Humanities, Natural Science, Social Science and Life Science. Students must score 60 points or higher in Mandarin Chinese (III) and (IV) before taking Mandarin Chinese (V) and (VI).</p><p>英語檢定English Testing（1）、經典五十Fifty Canonized Books（2）、服務學習Service Learning（1）</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td colspan="8"><p>體育除修習大一至大二4個學期外，另需通過「游泳能力檢定」及「心肺適能檢定」等二項檢測，列為畢業門檻。</p><p>Beside taking PE courses for 4 semesters (Year 1 to 2), students must pass both swimming and cardiopulmonary function tests.</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>通識教育科目General Education</p><p>（10）</p></td><td colspan="8"><p>通識課程分為人文藝術、自然科學、社會科學及生命科學四大類。學生須於四大領域中各選修2學分課程，共計8學分。General Education program comprises four categories：Humanities, Natural Science, Social Science and Life Science. Students require passing at least two 'digital application courses'. (Student may take 'digital application courses' from another department.)</p><ol><li>本系同學總共必須修滿 128學分方可畢業，包括共同必修及通識課程共31學分、本系必修35學分，選修62學分（外系選修至多承認24學分，與他系合作之學程，依學程規定承認最高學分）。</li></ol><p>Student of Dept. of Ad must take 128 credits in total for graduation,include Required Common Courses and General Education courses (31), Department Compulsory courses (35), and Department Elective courses (62). (Outside the Department of elective up to recognize the (24) credits, and the cooperation courses with other departments, according to the provisions of the highest recognition of credit)</p><ol><li>學生至少選擇「社區企劃」、「社會工作」、「政府行政」、「文化治理」四個領域中的二個領域，做為必選修課程模組，每一個模組至少完成三門課程。</li></ol><p>（1）「社區企劃」模組必選修課程包括：「台灣社會問題」、「社區組織與發展」、「非營利組織與管理」、「社會關懷與實踐」、「社會企業與社會創新」。</p><p>（2）「社會工作」模組必選修課程包括：「人類行為與社會環境」、「社會工作概論」、「社會政策與社會立法」、「社會福利概論」、「方案設計與評估」。</p><p>（3）「政府行政」模組必選修課程包括：「政治學」、「人力資源管理」、「行政法」、「政治經濟學專題」、「社會政策分析」。</p><p>（4）「文化治理」模組必選修課程包括：「文化研究概論」、「族群關係與多元文化政策 」、「台灣社會與文化研究」、「文化產業概論」、「文化政策」。</p><ol><li>建立社政系學習護照633（大學部6個學期，每學期參與3個系內活動(含1個工作坊、2個演講或活動)，另完成校內3個演講或活動(含外籍生 )。</li><li><strong>「為增進學生英文能力，鼓勵選修英語授課課程(含英專班)，其修習之課程科目及學分數之認抵需依學系規定辦理</strong>」</li></ol><p>To improve students’ English, we encourage students to take the courses in English (including  English Bachelor), which courses and credits waiver and transference should be standardized by each department.</p></td></tr></table>

AA-CP-04-CF02 (1.3 版)／102.04.19 修訂

Students must score 60 points or higher in Mandarin Chinese (III) and (IV) before taking Mandarin Chinese (V) and (VI).</p><p>英語檢定English Testing（1）、經典五十Fifty Canonized Books（2）、服務學習Service Learning（1）</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td><p>興趣選項體育optional physical education（0）</p></td><td><p>興趣選項體育optional physical education（0）</p></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td colspan="8"><p>大學部必須修習4學期體育課程；其中2學期為大一體育課程原班級上課，另2學期為興趣選項體育課程，另需通過「游泳能力檢定」及「心肺適能檢定」等二項檢測，列為畢業門檻。</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>通識教育科目General Education</p><p>（10）</p></td><td colspan="8"><p>The undergraduate students must attend the physical education course for 4 semesters; 2 semesters for the freshman physical education courses, the other two semesters for the optional physical education courses, students must pass both swimming and cardiopulmonary function tests.</p><p>通識課程分為人文藝術、自然科學、社會科學及生命科學四大類。學生須於四大領域中各選修2學分課程，共計8學分。General Education program comprises four categories：Humanities, Natural Science, Social Science and Life Science. required to take a 2-credit course from the four categories according to each college’s policy before (Outside the Department of elective up to recognize the (24) credits, and the cooperation courses with other departments, according to the provisions of the highest recognition of credit)</p><ol><li>學生至少選擇「社區企劃」、「社會工作」、「政府行政」、「文化治理」四個領域中的二個領域，做為必選修課程模組，每一個模組至少完成三門課程。</li></ol><p>（1）「社區企劃」模組必選修課程包括：「台灣社會問題」、「社區組織與發展」、「非營利組織與管理」、「社會關懷與實踐」、「社會企業與社會創新」。</p><p>（2）「社會工作」模組必選修課程包括：「人類行為與社會環境」、「社會工作概論」、「社會政策與社會立法」、「社會福利概論」、「方案設計與評估」。</p><p>（3）「政府行政」模組必選修課程包括：「政治學」、「人力資源管理」、「行政法」、「政治經濟學專題」、「社會政策分析」。</p><p>（4）「文化治理」模組必選修課程包括：「文化研究概論」、「族群關係與多元文化政策 」、「台灣社會與文化研究」、「文化產業概論」、「文化政策」。</p><ol><li>建立社政系學習護照633（大學部6個學期，每學期參與3個系內活動(含1個工作坊、2個演講或活動)，另完成校內3個演講或活動(含外籍生 )。</li><li><strong>「為增進學生英文能力，鼓勵選修英語授課課程(含英專班)，其修習之課程科目及學分數之認抵需依學系規定辦理</strong>」</li></ol><p>To improve students’ English, we encourage students to take the courses in English (including  English Bachelor), which courses and credits waiver and transference should be standardized by each department.</p></td></tr></table>

**元智大學 社會暨政策科學學系 必修科目表**

**Department of Social and Policy Sciences, Yuan Ze University**

**List of Required Courses**

**（111學年度入學新生適用）**

**(Applicable to Students Admitted in Academic Year of 2022)**

111.04.20 一一○學年度第六次教務會議通過

111.09.21 一一一學年度第一次教務會議修訂通過

Amended by the 1st Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2022, on September 21, 2022

114.12.24 一一四學年度第四次教務會議修訂通過

<table><tr><td rowspan="2"><p>學年Academic Year</p><p>學期Semester</p><p>科目Subject</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>第一學年1<sup>st</sup> Academic Year</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>第二學年2<sup>nd</sup> Academic Year</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>第三學年3<sup>rd</sup> Academic Year</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>第四學年4<sup>th</sup> Academic Year</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>上Fall</p></td><td><p>下Spring</p></td><td><p>上Fall</p></td><td><p>下Spring</p></td><td><p>上Fall</p></td><td><p>下Spring</p></td><td><p>上Fall</p></td><td><p>下Spring</p></td></tr><tr><td rowspan="7"><p>共同必修科目University Compulsory</p><p>（21）</p></td><td><p>國文（一）</p><p>Chinese (I)</p><p>（2）</p></td><td><p>國文（二）</p><p>Chinese (II)</p><p>（2）</p></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td><p>英語（一）</p><p>English (I)</p><p>（2）</p></td><td><p>英語（二）</p><p>English (II)</p><p>（2）</p></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td><p>基礎程式設計(一)</p><p>Fundamental Computer Programming (I)（2）</p></td><td><p>基礎程式設計(二)</p><p>Fundamental Computer Programming (Π)（2）</p></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td colspan="8"><p>程式語言共4學分，依各院修課規則辦理。(開課名稱：基礎程式設計(一)、基礎程式設計(二))</p><p>Fundamental Computer Programming is a four-credit course. For those who would like to registered “Fundamental computer programming”, he/she has to meet the college requirement. (Course Name: Fundamental Computer Programming(一)、Fundamental Computer Programming(二))</p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="8"><p>外語課程應修習10學分。</p><ol><li>「英語（一）」及「英語（二）」為基礎課程，採能力分級上課，共計二學期四學分。</li><li>除了「英語（一）」及「英語（二）」外，畢業前應修畢三個不同主題式英語課程，共三學期5學分。</li><li>大一英語能力後測「TOEIC模擬測驗」成績未達350分者，應修習「應試加強班」(EL260)。修習「應試加強班」期間之期末TOEIC模擬測驗成績未達350分者，則該科成績將「不及格」，並應再次修習「應試加強班」，直到取得TOEIC模擬測驗分數達350分(含)始得修習其他主題式英語課程。</li><li>另開設「英語檢定」(EL360)計一學期1學分，「英語檢定」之修課限制與注意事項，請參照「通識外語『英語檢定』修課規定」，並由通識教學部公佈後施行。</li></ol><p>外國學生改修華語須經國際語言文化中心審核通過始可改修華語課程10學分，其華語課程10學分應含「華語檢定」1學分，「華語檢定」修課限制與注意事項，請參照「通識外語『英語檢定』修課規定」。</p><p>凡本校大學部外國學生修習「華語(一)」或「華語(二)」任一課程成績未達60分，不得修習「華語(三)」、「華語(四)」。若修習「華語(三)」、「華語(四)」任一課程成績未達60分，不得修習「華語(五)」或「華語檢定」(EL372)。</p><p>The undergraduate students must complete 10 required credits of foreign language courses.</p><ol><li>English (I) &amp; (II) for the total 4 credits: English (I) and (II) are 4 credit elementary courses for the freshmen who are grouped on English competence; to complete within two semesters.</li><li>English thematic course for the total 5 credits: English thematic courses are 5-credit English courses; students are required to obtain 5 credits through 3 different thematic courses for graduation. </li><li>Students who do not reach the 350-point threshold of TOEIC Mock Exam in the end of the freshman year must take “English Testing” (EL260) course. Students will fail the course if they do not score higher than 350 points in TOEIC Mock Exam by the end of the course, and must repeatedly take the course until they can score higher than 350 points. </li><li>“English Testing” (EL360) for the total 1 credit: For the requirements of registering “English Testing”, please refer to "the Regulation for Registering English Test" announced and implemented by the College of General Education.</li></ol><p>Foreign students need approval by ILCC for taking 10 credits of Mandarin Chinese courses as alternative courses of English.</p><p>The undergraduate foreign students must pass Mandarin Chinese (I) and (II) before taking Mandarin Chinese (III) and (IV). Students must pass Mandarin Chinese (III) and (IV) before taking Mandarin Chinese (V) and Chinese Proficiency Test (EL372).</p><p>英語檢定English Testing（1）、經典五十Fifty Canonized Books（2）、服務學習Service Learning（1）</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td><p>興趣選項體育optional physical education（0）</p></td><td><p>興趣選項體育optional physical education（0）</p></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td colspan="8"><p>大學部必須修習4學期體育課程；其中2學期為大一體育課程原班級上課，另2學期為興趣選項體育課程。</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>通識教育科目General Education</p><p>（10）</p></td><td colspan="8"><p>The undergraduate students must attend the physical education course for 4 semesters; 2 semesters for the freshman physical education courses, the other two semesters for the optional physical education courses.</p><p>通識課程分為人文藝術、自然科學、社會科學及生命科學四大類。學生須於四大領域中各選修2學分課程，共計8學分。General Education program comprises four categories：Humanities, Natural Science, Social Science and Life Science. Students are required to take a 2-credit course from each category to get 8 credits before graduation.</p><p>通識跨域課程General Education Interdisciplinary Course：此2學分學生可自由於通識講座課程、微課自主學習或在地多元文化課群中選課。惟外籍生與工程學院英語學士班、資訊學院英語學士班、人文社會學院英語學士班、電機通訊學院英語學士班學生仍須於四大領域中選課，依各院修課規定辦理。Students can select the 2 credits from a General Education Lecture course, Micro Credit courses, Self-Study courses, or Local-Multicultural courses. Only foreign students and undergraduates of International Programs in the Colleges of Engineering, Informatics, Humanities and Social Sciences, as well as Electrical and Communication Engineering are required to take a 2-credit course from the four categories according to each college’s policy before Each of the first three department-organized talks or activities is counted as 25 points, while each additional talk or activity (whether within or outside the department) is counted as 10 points." </p></td></tr></table>

**元智大學 社會暨政策科學學系 必修科目表**

**Department of Social and Policy Sciences, Yuan Ze University**

**List of Required Courses**

**（112學年度入學新生適用）**

**(Applicable to Students Admitted in Academic Year of 2023)**

112.04.19 一一一學年度第六次教務會議通過

112.05.31 一一一學年度第七次教務會議通過

114.12.24 一一四學年度第四次教務會議修訂通過

115.04.29 一一四學年度第七次教務會議修訂通過

<table><tr><td rowspan="2"><p>學年Academic Year</p><p>學期Semester</p><p>科目Subject</p></td><td colspan="5"><p>第一學年1<sup>st</sup> Academic Year</p></td><td colspan="7"><p>第二學年2<sup>nd</sup> Academic Year</p></td><td colspan="6"><p>第三學年3<sup>rd</sup> Academic Year</p></td><td colspan="4"><p>第四學年4<sup>th</sup> Academic Year</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>上Fall</p></td><td colspan="4"><p>下Spring</p></td><td colspan="4"><p>上Fall</p></td><td colspan="3"><p>下Spring</p></td><td colspan="3"><p>上Fall</p></td><td colspan="3"><p>下Spring</p></td><td colspan="3"><p>上Fall</p></td><td><p>下Spring</p></td></tr><tr><td rowspan="5"><p>共同必修科目</p><p>University Compulsory</p><p>（17）</p></td><td><p>國文（一）</p><p>Chinese (I)</p><p>（2）</p></td><td colspan="4"><p>國文（二）</p><p>Chinese (II)</p><p>（2）</p></td><td colspan="4"></td><td colspan="3"></td><td colspan="3"></td><td colspan="3"></td><td colspan="3"></td><td></td></tr><tr><td><p>英語（一）</p><p>English (I)</p><p>（2）</p></td><td colspan="4"><p>英語（二）</p><p>English (II)</p><p>（2）</p></td><td colspan="4"></td><td colspan="3"></td><td colspan="3"></td><td colspan="3"></td><td colspan="3"></td><td></td></tr><tr><td colspan="22"><p>外語課程應修習10學分。</p><ol><li>「英語（一）」及「英語（二）」為基礎課程，採能力分級上課，共計二學期四學分。</li><li>除了「英語（一）」及「英語（二）」外，畢業前應修畢三個不同主題式英語課程，共三學期5學分。</li><li>大一英語能力後測「TOEIC模擬測驗」成績未達350分者，應修習「應試加強班」(EL260)。修習「應試加強班」期間之期末TOEIC模擬測驗成績未達350分者，則該科成績將「不及格」，並應再次修習「應試加強班」，直到取得TOEIC模擬測驗分數達350分(含)始得修習其他主題式英語課程。</li><li>另開設「英語檢定」(EL360)計一學期1學分，「英語檢定」之修課限制與注意事項，請參照「通識外語『英語檢定』修課規定」，並由通識教學部公佈後施行。</li></ol><p>外國學生改修華語須經國際語言文化中心審核通過始可改修華語課程10學分，其華語課程10學分應含「華語檢定」1學分，「華語檢定」修課限制與注意事項，請參照「通識外語『英語檢定』修課規定」。</p><p>凡本校大學部外國學生修習「華語（一）」或「華語（二）」任一課程成績未達60分，不得修習「華語（三）」、「華語（四）」。若修習「華語（三）」、「華語（四）」任一課程成績未達60分，不得修習「華語（五）」或「華語檢定」（EL372）。</p><p>The undergraduate students must complete 10 required credits of foreign language courses.</p><ol><li>English (I) &amp; (II) for the total 4 credits: English (I) and (II) are 4 credit elementary courses for the freshmen who are grouped on English competence; to complete within two semesters.</li><li>English thematic course for the total 5 credits: English thematic courses are 5-credit English courses; students are required to obtain 5 credits through 3 different thematic courses for graduation. </li><li>Students who do not reach the 350-point threshold of TOEIC Mock Exam in the end of the freshman year must take “English Testing” (EL260) course. Students will fail the course if they do not score higher than 350 points in TOEIC Mock Exam by the end of the course, and must repeatedly take the course until they can score higher than 350 points. </li><li>“English Testing” (EL360) for the total 1 credit: For the requirements of registering “English Testing”, please refer to "the Regulation for Registering English Test" announced and implemented by the College of General Education.</li></ol><p>Foreign students need approval by ILCC for taking 10 credits of Mandarin Chinese courses as alternative courses of English.</p><p>The undergraduate foreign students must pass Mandarin Chinese (I) and (II) before taking Mandarin Chinese (III) and (IV). Students must pass Mandarin Chinese (III) and (IV) before taking Mandarin Chinese (V) and Chinese Proficiency Test (EL372).</p><p>英語檢定English Testing（1）、經典選讀A Guide to Classics（2）、服務學習Service Learning（1）</p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="2"><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td colspan="3"><p>興趣選項體育optional physical education（0）</p></td><td colspan="3"><p>興趣選項體育optional physical education（0）</p></td><td colspan="3"></td><td colspan="3"></td><td colspan="3"></td><td colspan="3"></td></tr><tr><td colspan="22"><p>大學部必須修習4學期體育課程；其中2學期為大一體育課程原班級上課，另2學期為興趣選項體育課程。</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>通識教育科目General Education</p><p>（10）</p></td><td colspan="22"><p>The undergraduate students must attend the physical education course for 4 semesters; 2 semesters for the freshman physical education courses, the other two semesters for the optional physical education courses.</p><p>通識課程分為人文藝術、自然科學、社會科學及生命科學四大類。學生須於四大領域中各選修2學分課程，共計8學分。General Education program comprises four categories：Humanities, Natural Science, Social Science and Life Science. Students are required to take a 2-credit course from each category to get 8 credits before graduation.</p><p>通識跨域課程General Education Interdisciplinary Course：此2學分學生可自由於通識講座課程、微課自主學習或在地多元文化課群中選課。惟外籍生與工程學院英語學士班、資訊學院英語學士班、人文社會學院英語學士班、電機通訊學院英語學士班學生仍須於四大領域中選課，依各院修課規定辦理。Students can select the 2 credits from a General Education Lecture course, Micro Credit courses, Self-Study courses, or Local-Multicultural courses. Only foreign students and undergraduates of International Programs in the Colleges of Engineering, Informatics, Humanities and Social Sciences, as well as Electrical and Communication Engineering are required to take a 2-credit course from the four categories according to each college’s policy before graduation.</p><p>通識4大領域各選修2學分共計8學分，其餘2學分之通識跨域課程改為「必選修｣，可於通識講座課程、微課自主學習或在地多元文化課群中選課，亦即不可由四大領域中選課。</p><p>必修社會科學領域:法學緒論2學分。Compulsory Social Sciences Courses: Introduction to Law, 2 Credits</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>院必修科目</p><p>College</p><p>Compulsory</p><p>（4）</p></td><td colspan="22"><p>程式語言共4學分，依各院修課規則辦理。</p><p>The Fundamental Computer Programming has 4 credits in total, which is subject to the rules of each college.</p><p>基礎程式設計（一） Fundamental Computer Programming (I)（2）(課號:HS002)、基礎程式設計（二） Fundamental Computer Programmin (Π)（2）(課號:HS003)</p></td></tr><tr><td rowspan="4"><p>系必修科目Department Compulsory</p><p> (35)</p></td><td colspan="3"><p>SC133</p><p>社會學</p><p>Sociology </p><p>（3）</p></td><td colspan="3"><p>SC219</p><p>社會心理學</p><p>Social Psychology The military education courses will not be accumulated to the graduation requirements, but they can be counted as taken credits for each semester.</p><ol><li>學生選修課程模組分類：「社會/政府行政」、「社會工作」、「社會企劃」三大軸向，各含有核心與精選次課程模組。學生須選修二核心課程模組與二精選課程模組各三門課。相關選修課程模組分類表請參閱「社會暨政策科學學系選修課程模組」。</li></ol><p>There are three focused, selective course dimensions towards the fields of social/governmental administration, social work, and social planning. Each dimension contains a core course module and a featured course module. Students must take two core modules and three courses each from two featured modules to fulfill graduation requirements.</p><ol><li>學生必須參與演講或活動才能取得職涯發展課程（一）至（六）的成績。前三場系內演講或活動每場計25分，其餘活動（無論系內或系外）每場計10分。</li></ol><p>Students must attend talks or activities to earn grades for The Development of Career (I), (II), (III), (IV), (V), and (VI) courses. Each of the first three department-organized talks or activities is counted as 25 points, while each additional talk or activity (whether within or outside the department) is counted as 10 points."  </p></td></tr></table>

AA-CP-04-CF02 (1.4版)／113.12.16修訂
```

**Department of Social and Policy Sciences, Yuan Ze University**

**List of Required Courses**

115.04.29 一一四學年度第七次教務會議修訂通過

（II） for the total 4 credits: English （I） and （II） are 4 credits elementary courses for the freshmen who are grouped on English competence; to complete within two semesters.</li><li>English thematic course for the total 4 credits: English thematic courses are 4-credit English courses; students are required to obtain 4 credits through 2 different thematic courses for graduation. </li><li>Students who do not reach the 350-point threshold of TOEIC Mock Exam in the end of the freshman year must take English Testing （EL260） course. Students will fail the course if they do not score higher than 350 points of TOEIC Mock Exam by the end of the course, and must repeatedly take the course until they can score higher than 350 points. </li><li>“English Testing” （EL160） is a 2-credit course: For the requirements of registering “English Testing”, please refer to The Regulation for Registering English Test announced and implemented by the College of General Education.</li><li>Foreign students need approval by ILCC for taking 10 credits of Mandarin Chinese courses as alternative courses of English. The 10 credits in Mandarin Chinese courses must include 2 credits for “Chinese Proficiency Test”. For the specific restrictions and considerations for taking the “Chinese Proficiency Test”, please refer to the 'General Education Foreign Language “English Proficiency Exam” Course Requirements' and 'Yuan Ze University Regulations for Exempting the Mandarin Chinese as a Foreign Language Credit ' for more details.</li><li>The undergraduate foreign students must pass Mandarin Chinese (I) and (II) before taking Mandarin Chinese (III) and (IV). Students must pass Mandarin Chinese (III) and (IV) before taking 'Chinese Proficiency Test' （EL375）.</li></ol><p> 英語檢定English Testing （2）、經典選讀A Guide to Classics （2）、服務學習Service Learning （1）</p><ol><li>修習「經典選讀」課程，2學分，大二以上修習。tudents are required to take a 2-credit course “A Guide to Classics”。</li><li>必修一學分，大學部學生由大一開始至大四結束前，修滿18小時之服務學習課程與18小時之服務學習活動，得於大四畢業前取得學分，課程與活動分各院系、通識教學部、教務處、學生事務處等單位開辦，課程與活動清單請參考個人PORTAL之服務學習系統。<br/>YZU Service-Learning takes up one credit learning for mandatory learning as undergraduates. Each student has to finish 18 hours of learning and 18 hours of activity before the end of their senior year. All Service-Learning curriculum and activities could refer to Service-Learning System of portal.</li></ol></td></tr><tr><td><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>興趣選項體育optional physical education（0）</p></td><td><p>興趣選項體育optional physical education（0）</p></td><td colspan="2"></td><td></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td colspan="10"><p>大學部必須修習4學期體育課程；其中2學期為大一體育課程原班級上課，另2學期為興趣選項體育課程。</p><p>The undergraduate students must attend the physical education course for 4 semesters; 2 semesters for the freshman physical education courses, the other two semesters for the optional physical education courses.</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>通識教育科目</p><p>General Education（10）</p></td><td colspan="10"><p>通識課程分為人文藝術、自然科學、社會科學及生命科學四大類。學生須於四大領域中各選修2學分課程，共計8學分。General Education program comprises four categories：Humanities, Natural Science, Social Science and Life Science. Students are required to take a 2-credit course from each category to get 8 credits before graduation.</p><p>通識跨域課程General Education Interdisciplinary Course：此2學分學生可自由於通識講座課程、微課自主學習或在地多元文化課群中選課。惟外籍生與工程學院英語學士班、資訊學院英語學士班、人文社會學院英語學士班、電機通訊學院英語學士班學生仍須於四大領域中選課，依各院修課規定辦理。Students can select the 2 credits from a General Education Lecture course, Micro Credit courses, Self-Study courses, or Local-Multicultural courses. required to take a 2-credit course from the four categories according to each college’s policy before courses".</p><ol><li>「大數據與政策分析應用基礎」課程（課號SC132）、「大數據與政策分析應用進階」課程(課號SC249)為本系「數位應用相關課程｣，畢業前須通過至少2門「數位應用相關課程」(可至本系或外系修習)。(通識程式語言課程為本校發展「數位跨域」的基礎課程，不重複列為每位學生必須修習的兩門「數位應用相關課程」。資訊概論、計算機概論、網路概論等課程不可列入「數位應用相關課程」，須強調利用數位技術，實作出數位作品。)</li></ol><p>“Big Data and Policy Analysis Application Basic (course code SC132)”, and “Big Data and Policy Analysis Advanced (course code SC249)” are courses of “digital application courses.” Students are required to take and pass at least two “digital application courses.” (Student may take “digital application courses” from another department.)</p><ol><li>本系同學總共必須修滿 128學分方可畢業，包括共同必修及通識課程共27學分、院必修數位人文應用課程共4學分、本系必修35學分，選修62學分（外系選修至多承認24學分，與他系合作之學程，依學程規定承認最高學分）。</li></ol><p>Student of Department of Social and Policy Sciences are required to accomplished 128 credits in total for graduation, including 27 credits for required common courses and general education courses, 4 credits for college compulsory courses--fundamental computer programming, 35 credits for the departmental compulsory courses, and 62 additional credits for elective courses among which students are allowed to take up to 24 credits of courses from other departments.</p><p>(Outside the Department of elective up to recognize the (24 credits), and the cooperation courses with other departments, according to the provisions of the highest recognition of credit)</p><ol><li>為增進學生英文能力，鼓勵選修英語授課課程(含英專班)，其修習之課程科目及學分數之認抵需依學系規定辦理。</li></ol><p>To improve students’ English, we encourage students to take the courses in English (including English Bachelor), which courses and credits waiver and transference should be standardized by each department.</p><ol><li>自106學年度起軍訓課程由必修改為選修，該學分納入當學期修課學分數計算，但不納入畢業總學分計算。</li></ol><p>The military education courses are no longer compulsory starting the 106 academic year. The military education courses will not be accumulated to the graduation requirements, but they can be counted as taken credits for each semester.</p><ol><li>修習碩士班課程以大三以上學生為限，且不得修習碩士在職專班課程。</li></ol><p>Master's degree courses are limited to students in their third year or above, and students are not allowed to take courses from the Executive Master program.</p><ol><li>學生選修課程模組分類：「社會/政府行政」、「社會工作」、「社會企劃」三大軸向，各含有核心與精選次課程模組。學生須選修二核心課程模組與二精選課程模組各三門課。相關選修課程模組分類表請參閱「社會暨政策科學學系選修課程模組」。</li></ol><p>There are three focused, selective course dimensions towards the fields of social/governmental administration, social work, and social planning. Each dimension contains a core course module and a featured course module. Students must take two core modules and three courses each from two featured modules to fulfill graduation requirements.</p><ol><li>學生必須參與演講或活動才能取得職涯發展課程（一）至（六）的成績。前三場系內演講或活動每場計25分，其餘活動（無論系內或系外）每場計10分。</li></ol><p>Students must attend talks or activities to earn grades for The Development of Career (I), (II), (III), (IV), (V), and (VI) courses. Each of the first three department-organized talks or activities is counted as 25 points, while each additional talk or activity (whether within or outside the department) is counted as 10 points." </p></td></tr></table>

**元智大學 社會暨政策科學學系 選修科目表**

YZU Social and Policy Sciences Elective Course Chart

**（113學年度入學新生適用Academic Year 2024）**

113.05.01 一一二學年度第八次教務會議通過

**Department of Social and Policy Sciences, Yuan Ze University**

**List of Required Courses**

**（114學年度入學新生適用）**

114.12.24 一一四學年度第四次教務會議修訂通過

115.04.29 一一四學年度第七次教務會議修訂通過

The undergraduate students must complete 10 required credits of foreign language courses.</p><p>2.	English (I) &amp; (II) for the total 4 credits: English (I) and (II) are 4 credits elementary courses for the freshmen who are grouped on English competence; to complete within two semesters.</p><p>3.	English thematic course for the total 4 credits: English thematic courses are 4-credit English courses; students are required to obtain 4 credits through 2 different thematic courses for graduation. </p><p>4.	Students who do not reach the 350-point threshold of TOEIC Mock Exam in the end of the freshman year must take English Testing (EL260) course. Students will fail the course if they do not score higher than 350 points of TOEIC Mock Exam by the end of the course, and must repeatedly take the course until they can score higher than 350 points. </p><p>5.	“English Testing” (EL160) is a 2-credit course: For the requirements of registering “English Testing”, please refer to The Regulation for Registering English Test announced and implemented by the College of General Education.</p><p>6.	Foreign students could take 10 credits of Mandarin Chinese courses as alternative courses of English.<strong> </strong>The 10 credits in Mandarin Chinese courses must include 2 credits for “Chinese Proficiency Test”. For the specific restrictions and considerations for taking the “Chinese Proficiency Test”, please refer to the 'General Education Foreign Language “English Proficiency Exam” Course Requirements' and 'Yuan Ze University Regulations for Exempting the Mandarin Chinese as a Foreign Language Credit ' for more details.</p><p>7. The undergraduate foreign students must pass Mandarin Chinese (I) and (II) before taking Mandarin Chinese (III) and (IV). Students must pass Mandarin Chinese (III) and (IV) before taking 'Chinese Proficiency Test' (EL375).</p><p> 英語檢定English Testing（2）、經典選讀A Guide to Classics（2）、服務學習Service Learning（1） </p></td></tr><tr><td><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td><p>興趣選項體育optional physical education（0）</p></td><td><p>興趣選項體育optional physical education（0）</p></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td colspan="8"><p>大學部必須修習4學期體育課程；其中2學期為大一體育課程原班級上課，另2學期為興趣選項體育課程。</p><p>The undergraduate students must attend the physical education course for 4 semesters; 2 semesters for the freshman physical education courses, the other two semesters for the optional physical education courses.</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>通識教育科目</p><p>General Education（10）</p></td><td colspan="8"><p>通識課程分為人文藝術、自然科學、社會科學及生命科學四大類。學生須於四大領域中各選修2學分課程，共計8學分。General Education program comprises four categories：Humanities, Natural Science, Social Science and Life Science. Students are required to take a 2-credit course from each category to get 8 credits before graduation.</p><p>通識跨域課程General Education Interdisciplinary Course：此2學分學生可自由於通識講座課程、微課自主學習或在地多元文化課群中選課。惟外籍生與工程學院英語學士班、資訊學院英語學士班、人文社會學院英語學士班、電機通訊學院英語學士班學生仍須於四大領域中選課，依各院修課規定辦理。Students can select the 2 credits from a General Education Lecture course, Micro Credit courses, Self-Study courses, or Local-Multicultural courses. Only foreign students and undergraduates of International Programs in the Colleges of Engineering, Informatics, Humanities and Social Sciences, as well as Electrical and Communication Engineering are required to take a 2-credit course from the four categories according to each college’s policy before graduation.</p><p>通識4大領域各選修2學分共計8學分，其餘2學分之通識跨域課程改為「必選修｣，可於通識講座課程、微課自主學習或在地多元文化課群中選課，亦即不可由四大領域中選課。</p><p>必修社會科學領域:法學緒論2學分。Compulsory Social Sciences Courses: Introduction to Law, 2 Credits taken in excess of the general education department (including the International Language Center) will not be counted as graduation credits.</p><ol><li>終端學習課程： SC406實地工作 （實習）（二）<strong> </strong>The experiential learning courses.</li><li>政策規劃與執行課程（課號SC432）為本系必修「議題導向實作專題課程」3學分. </li></ol><p>Policy Planning and implementation（Course code SC432） is a compulsory three-credit course of "Topic and Implementation-oriented courses".</p><ol><li>「大數據與政策分析應用基礎」課程（課號SC132）、「大數據與政策分析應用進階」課程(課號SC249)為本系「數位應用相關課程｣，畢業前須通過至少2門「數位應用相關課程」（可至本系或外系修習）。   “Big Data and Policy Analysis Application Basic (course code SC132)”, and “Big Data and Policy Analysis Advanced (course code SC249)”are courses of 'digital application courses'. Students require passing at least two 'digital application courses'. （Student may take 'digital application courses' from another department.）</li><li>本系同學總共必須修滿 128學分方可畢業，包括共同必修及通識課程共27學分、院必修程式語言課程共4學分、本系必修37學分，選修60學分（自由選修至多承認24學分，含專業自主學習1學分。與他系合作之學程，依學程規定承認最高學分）。</li></ol><p>Student of Dept. of Ad must take 128 credits in total for graduation, include Required Common Courses and General Education courses（27）credits , College Compulsory Courses Fundamental Computer Programming（4）credits , Department Compulsory courses（37）credits, and Department Elective courses（60）credits.（A maximum of （24） credits can be recognized for free electives, including（1）credit for disciplinary self-directed learning. For the cooperation courses with other departments, credits will be recognized according to the specific program regulations.）</p><ol><li>為增進學生英文能力，鼓勵選修英語授課課程（含英專班），其修習之課程科目及學分數之認抵需依學系規定辦理。</li></ol><p>To improve students’English, we encourage students to take the courses in English（including English Bachelor）, which courses and credits waiver and transference should be standardized by each department.</p><ol><li>自106學年度起軍訓課程由必修改為選修，該學分納入當學期修課學分數計算，但不納入畢業總學分計算。</li></ol><p>The military education courses are no longer compulsory starting the 106 academic year. The military education courses will not be accumulated to the graduation requirements, but they can be counted as taken credits for each semester.</p><ol><li>修習碩士班課程以大三以上學生為限，且不得修習碩士在職專班課程。</li></ol><p>Master's degree courses are limited to students in their third year or above, and students are not allowed to take courses from the Executive Master program.</p><ol><li>學生選修課程模組分類：「社會/政府行政」、「社會工作」、「社會企劃」三大軸向，各含有核心與精選次課程模組。學生須選修二核心課程模組與二精選課程模組各三門課。相關選修課程模組分類表請參閱「社會暨政策科學學系選修課程模組」。</li></ol><p>There are three focused, selective course dimensions towards the fields of social/governmental administration, social work, and social planning. Each dimension contains a core course module and a featured course module. Students must take two core modules and three courses each from two featured modules to fulfill graduation requirements.</p><ol><li>學生必須參與演講或活動才能取得職涯發展課程（一）至（六）的成績。前三場系內演講或活動每場計25分，其餘活動（無論系內或系外）每場計10分。</li></ol><p>Students must attend talks or activities to earn grades for The Development of Career (I), (II), (III), (IV), (V), and (VI) courses. Each of the first three department-organized talks or activities is counted as 25 points, while each additional talk or activity (whether within or outside the department) is counted as 10 points." </p></td></tr></table>

AA-CP-04-CF02 (1.4版)／113.12.16修訂
```

- 本機檔案: admin/aa/files/COURSES/604SC/106SC-3.docx

```markdown
**元智大學 社會暨政策科學學系 擋修科目表**

YZU Social and Policy Sciences Restricted Course Chart

**（106學年度入學新生適用）**

for students enrolling at the Academic Year 106

106.04.26 一○五學年度第五次教務會議通過

106.06.21 一○五學年度第六次教務會議修訂通過

109.05.06一○八學年度第六次教務會議修訂通過

<table><tr><td colspan="2"><p>先修科目Prerequisite Courses</p></td><td><p>擋修科目Restricted Courses</p></td><td rowspan="2"><p>備註Remarks</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>課名Course Name</p></td><td><p>分數Credits</p></td><td><p>課名Course Name</p></td></tr><tr><td rowspan="2"><p>社會學Sociology</p></td><td rowspan="2"><p>60</p></td><td><p>社會學理論Ι(上)</p><p>Sociological Theory Ι</p></td><td></td></tr><tr><td><p>社會學理論Ⅱ(下)</p><p>Sociological Theory Ⅱ</p></td><td></td></tr><tr><td><p>實地工作（實習）I</p><p>Internship Practice(I)</p></td><td><p>60</p></td><td><p>實地工作（實習）II Internship Practice(II)</p></td><td></td></tr><tr><td><p>實地工作（實習）II Internship Practice(II)</p></td><td><p>70</p></td><td><p>實地工作 （實習）Ⅲ</p><p>Field Practice(III)</p></td><td></td></tr></table>

- 依元智大學學則第二十一條規定：「學生所修全年之科目，其上學期成績不及格在四十分以上者，得准繼續修習下學期科目，其下學期及格者，學分照計，上學期不及格科目仍應重修。」故本系必選修課程，凡分上、下學期開設，上學期未達40分者，不得續修下學期。
- 分（上）、（下）之課程，均需先修習（上），始得修習（下）。
- 社會學達60分，始得修習社會學理論(上)、(下)。
- 實地工作（實習）I達60分，始得修習實地工作（實習）II。
- 實地工作（實習）II達70分，始得修習實地工作（實習）Ⅲ。
- 轉學生經授課教師及系主任同意，得同時修社會學與社會學理論。

- According to Yuan Ze University’s Academic Regulations, Article 21: “For all of a student’s courses, if a course is not passed but receives a grade above 40, the course shall be taken again the following semester. If the course is then passed, credits will be awarded accordingly. Failed courses should be repeated in the subsequent semester.” Therefore, if credit received for a required course that spans two semesters is less than 40 in the first semester, students will not be permitted to continue with the course in the following semester.
- courses marked “(I), (II),” students must complete course (I) before attempting course (II).
- Students must complete 60 credits of Sociology  before attempting Sociological Theory
- Students must complete 60 credits of Internship Practice (I) before attempting Internship Practice (II).
- Students must complete 70 credits of Internship Practice (II) before attempting Field Practice(III).
- With the approval of the course instructor and department head, transfer students may attempt Sociology and Sociological Theory courses simultaneously.
```

#### OCR 65: files/COURSES/604SC/108SC-3.docx

- 關聯類型: 超連結（檔案）
- 本機檔案: admin/aa/files/COURSES/604SC/108SC-3.docx
- OCR Markdown: /mnt/project/cache/ocr_completed_cache/ocr_md_assets/eeedacc8cfa4b360_108SC-3.md
- OCR 狀態: completed_cached
- OCR 字數: 2161
- 驗證狀態: ok

```markdown
**元智大學 社會暨政策科學學系 擋修科目表**

YZU Social and Policy Sciences Restricted Course Chart

**（108學年度入學新生適用）**

for students enrolling at the Academic Year 2019

108.05.01 一○七學年度第六次教務會議通過

109.05.06一○八學年度第六次教務會議修訂通過

110.11.24 一一○學年度第二次教務會議修訂通過

<table><tr><td colspan="2"><p>先修科目Prerequisite Courses</p></td><td><p>擋修科目Restricted Courses</p></td><td rowspan="2"><p>備註Remarks</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>課名Course Name</p></td><td><p>分數Credits</p></td><td><p>課名Course Name</p></td></tr><tr><td rowspan="2"><p>社會學Sociology</p></td><td rowspan="2"><p>60</p></td><td><p>社會學理論 (上)</p><p>Sociological Theory Ι</p></td><td></td></tr><tr><td><p>社會學理論 (下)</p><p>Sociological Theory Ⅱ</p></td><td></td></tr><tr><td><p>實地工作（實習）I</p><p>Internship Practice (I)</p></td><td><p>60</p></td><td><p>實地工作（實習）II Internship Practice (II)</p></td><td></td></tr><tr><td><p>實地工作（實習）II Internship Practice (II)</p></td><td><p>70</p></td><td><p>實地工作（實習）Ⅲ</p><p>Field Practice (III)</p></td><td></td></tr></table>

- 依元智大學學則第二十一條規定：「學生所修全年之科目，其上學期成績不及格在四十分以上者，得准繼續修習下學期科目，其下學期及格者，學分照計，上學期不及格科目仍應重修。」故本系必選修課程，凡分上、下學期開設，上學期未達40分者，不得續修下學期。
- 分（上）、（下）之課程，均需先修習（上），始得修習（下）。
- 社會學達60分，始得修習社會學理論(上)、(下)。
- 實地工作（實習）I達60分，始得修習實地工作（實習）II。
- 實地工作（實習）II達70分，始得修習實地工作（實習）Ⅲ。

- According to Yuan Ze University’s Academic Regulations, Article 21: “For all of a student’s courses, if a course is not passed but receives a grade above 40, the course shall be taken again the following semester. If the course is then passed, credits will be awarded accordingly. Failed courses should be repeated in the subsequent semester.” Therefore, if credit received for a required course that spans two semesters is less than 40 in the first semester, students will not be permitted to continue with the course in the following semester.
- courses marked “(I), (II),” students must complete course (I) before attempting course (II).
- Students must complete 60 credits of Sociology  before attempting Sociological Theory
- Students must complete 60 credits of Internship Practice (I) before attempting Internship Practice (II).
- Students must complete 70 credits of Internship Practice (II) before attempting Field Practice(III).
```

<!-- OCR_END -->

for students enrolling at the Academic Year 2022

114.11.12 一一四學年度第三次教務會議修訂通過

<table><tr><td colspan="2"><p>先修科目Prerequisite Courses</p></td><td><p>擋修科目Restricted Courses</p></td><td rowspan="2"><p>備註Remarks</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>課名Course Name</p></td><td><p>學分數Credits</p></td><td><p>課名Course Name</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>實地工作（實習）（一）</p><p>Internship Practice (I)</p></td><td><p>1</p></td><td><p>實地工作（實習）（二） Internship Practice (II)</p></td><td></td></tr><tr><td><p>實地工作（實習）（二）Internship Practice (II)</p></td><td><p>4</p></td><td><p>實地工作 （實習）（三）</p><p>Field Practice (III)</p></td><td></td></tr></table>

- 依元智大學學則第二十一條規定：「學生所修全年之科目，其上學期成績不及格在四十分以上者，得准繼續修習下學期科目，其下學期及格者，學分照計，上學期不及格科目仍應重修。」
- 分（上）、（下）之課程，均需先修習（上），始得修習（下）。
- 實地工作（實習）（一）達60分，始得修習實地工作（實習）（二）。
- 實地工作（實習）（二）達60分，始得修習實地工作（實習）（三）。

※    According to Yuan Ze University’s Academic Regulations, Article 21: “Students who enroll in a

course that requires a full academic year to complete but fail a first-semester course with a score of

40 or higher can still continue taking the course in the second semester. The second-semester grade

will be recognized if students earn a passing grade; students who fail the first-semester course shall

retake that course and earn a passing grade.

※    For courses marked (I) or (II), students must complete course (I) before taking course (II).

※    A score of 60 or above in Internship Practice (I) is required before taking Internship Practice (II).

※    A score of 60 or above in Internship Practice (II) is required before taking Field Practice (III).
```

```markdown
**元智大學 社會暨政策科學學系 擋修科目表**

YZU Social and Policy Sciences Restricted Course Chart

**（114學年度入學新生適用）**

for students enrolling at the Academic Year 2025

114.04.23 一一三學年度第五次教務會議通通

114.11.12 一一四學年度第三次教務會議修訂通過

115.04.29 一一四學年度第七次教務會議修訂通過

<table><tr><td colspan="2"><p>先修科目Prerequisite Courses</p></td><td><p>擋修科目Restricted Courses</p></td><td rowspan="2"><p>備註Remarks</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>課名Course Name</p></td><td><p>學分數Credits</p></td><td><p>課名Course Name</p></td></tr><tr><td rowspan="2"><p>實地工作（實習）（一）</p><p>Internship Practice (I)</p></td><td><p>1</p></td><td><p>實地工作（實習）（二） Internship Practice (II)</p></td><td></td></tr><tr><td><p>1</p></td><td><p>實地工作 （實習）（三）</p><p>Field Practice (III)</p></td><td></td></tr></table>

- 依元智大學學則第二十一條規定：「學生所修全年之科目，其上學期成績不及格在四十分以上者，得准繼續修習下學期科目，其下學期及格者，學分照計，上學期不及格科目仍應重修。」
- 分（上）、（下）之課程，均需先修習（上），始得修習（下）。
- 實地工作（實習）（一）達60分，始得修習實地工作（實習）（二）、實地工作（實習）（三）。

※    According to Yuan Ze University’s Academic Regulations, Article 21: “Students who enroll in a

course that requires a full academic year to complete but fail a first-semester course with a score of

40 or higher can still continue taking the course in the second semester. The second-semester grade

will be recognized if students earn a passing grade; students who fail the first-semester course shall

retake that course and earn a passing grade.

※    For courses marked (I) or (II), students must complete course (I) before taking course (II).

※    A score of 60 or above in Internship Practice (I) is required before taking Internship Practice (II).

and Field Practice (III).
```

## 元智大學社會學系輔系規定

90.05.09 八十九學年度第六次教務會議通過

◆ 申請資格及規定

1.須為二年級生以上。

2.申請前各學期學業成績總平均需達七十八分以上，且操行成績八十分以上者。

3.選修本系為輔系之學生必須滿30(含)學分以上，才予承認其輔系資格。

4.若必修科目與原修學系課程科目重覆者，得申請以本科目表選修及其他所列科目取代之，但核准後仍需修滿30學分，始承認其輔系資格。

元智大學社會學系輔系科目表

元智大學輔系科目表

YZU Social and Policy Sciences Minor Course Chart

（109學年度申請適用）

for students enrolling at the Academic Year 2020

109.05.06 一○八學年度第六次教務會議通過

◆申請資格及規定

1.申請前各學期學業成績總平均應達七十分以上。

2.選修本系為輔系之學生必須滿30(含)學分以上，才予承認其輔系資格。

3.若必修科目與原修學系課程科目重覆者，得申請以本科目表選修及其他所列科

目取代之，但核准後仍需修滿30學分，始承認其輔系資格。

◆Application Eligibility and Requirements

1. The applicant must have maintained an academic average each semester of at least 70.

2. Students minoring in this department must complete at least 30 credits to fulfill the minor requirement.

3. If compulsory courses for the student’s minor overlap with those for the major, the student must use this form to apply for recognition of such courses toward both requirements, and to select an additional elective course. After authorization, students must still complete at least 30 credits to fulfill the minor requirement.

```markdown
元智大學社會暨政策科學學系輔系科目表

Minor Course List for the Department of Social and Policy Sciences, Yuan Ze University

（適用於2023學年入學）

Applicable for the 2023 Academic Year Enrollment

112.04.19 一一一學年度第六次教務會議通過

112.11.22 一一二學年度第五次教務會議修訂通過

Amended by the 5th Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2023, on November 22, 2023

◆	申請資格及規定

1.	申請前各學期學業成績總平均應達七十分以上。

2.	選修本系為輔系之學生須至少修滿26學分，含完成必修18學分，及完成1個核心模組，始得承認其輔系資格。

3.	若必修科目與原修學系課程科目重覆者，得申請以社政系科目表選修及其他所列科目取代之，惟核准後仍需修滿26學分，始得承認其輔系資格。

◆	Qualifications and Regulations for Application

1. Applicants are required to have an overall average of at least 70 points or above in their academic grades for each semester prior to the application.

2. Students who choose the Department of Social and Policy Sciences as a minor are required to complete a minimum of 26 credits, including 18 credits of required courses and the completion of 1 core module, in order to be recognized as having a minor qualification.

3. If there are overlapping courses between required courses and the curriculum of the original major, students may apply to replace them with courses from the Department of Social and Policy Sciences and other listed subjects. However, even after approval, they still need to complete a minimum of 26 credits in order to be recognized as having a minor qualification.

The elective courses are categorized into the following modules. Students are required to select one core course module (8-9 credits).

```markdown
元智大學社會暨政策科學學系雙主修科目表

Dual Major Course List for the Department of Social and Policy Sciences, Yuan Ze University

（適用於112學年入學）

Applicable for the 2023 Academic Year Enrollment

112.06.20 一一一學年度第十七次系務會議新訂

113.06.05 一一二學年度第九次教務會議修訂通過

◆申請資格及規定

1.	申請前各學期學業成績總平均應達七十分以上。

2.	選修社政系雙主修之學生須至少修滿43學分，含35個必修學分及1個核心模組課程，始得承認其雙主修資格。

3.	若必修科目與原修學系課程科目重覆者，得申請以社政系科目表選修及其他所列科目取代之，惟核准後仍須至少修滿43學分，始得承認其雙主修資格。

◆	Qualifications and Regulations for Application

1. Applicants are required to have an overall average of at least 70 points or above in their academic grades for each semester prior to the application.

2. Students pursuing a dual major in the Department of Social and Policy Sciences must complete a minimum of 43 credits, including 18 compulsory credits plus 2 core module courses, and 1 elective module course, in order to be recognized as having dual major qualifications.

3. If there are overlapping courses between required courses and the curriculum of the original major, students may apply to replace them with courses from the Department of Social and Policy Sciences and other listed subjects. However, even after approval, they still need to complete a minimum of 43 credits to be eligible for dual major status.

註：各科擋修科目，請參考擋修科目表（含上擋修下的科目）規定。

Note: Please refer to the prerequisite course table for the blocking requirements of each subject.

```markdown
元智大學社會暨政策科學學系雙主修科目表

Dual Major Course List for the Department of Social and Policy Sciences, Yuan Ze University

（適用於113學年入學）

Applicable for the 2024 Academic Year Enrollment

113.06.05 一一二學年度第九次教務會議通過

◆申請資格及規定

1.	申請前各學期學業成績總平均應達七十分以上。

2.	選修社政系雙主修之學生應修必修科目與學分須至少修滿43學分，含35個必修學分及1個核心模組課程，始得承認其雙主修資格。

3.	若必修科目與原修學系課程科目重覆者，得申請以社政系科目表選修及其他所列科目取代之，惟核准後仍須至少修滿43學分，始得承認其雙主修資格。

◆	Qualifications and Regulations for Application

1. Applicants are required to have an overall average of at least 70 points or above in their academic grades for each semester prior to the application.

2. Students pursuing a dual major in the Department of Social and Policy Sciences must complete a minimum of 43 credits, including 18 compulsory credits plus 2 core module courses, and 1 elective module course, in order to be recognized as having dual major qualifications.

3. If there are overlapping courses between required courses and the curriculum of the original major, students may apply to replace them with courses from the Department of Social and Policy Sciences and other listed subjects. However, even after approval, they still need to complete a minimum of 43 credits to be eligible for dual major status.

A minimum of 30 credits are required for graduation, in addition to a master’s thesis. Master students should select their thesis topic at least two weeks before their first year of study.</p><p>2. This degree program’s course requirements include:</p><ol><li> Compulsory courses: 12 credits</li><li> Elective courses: 18 credits (this department requires at least 9 elective credits)</li></ol><p>3. Regular students’ elective courses will not be credited toward vocational course requirements.</p><p>4. If the investigation and qualitative research were repaired, of which three credits for compulsory credits, the other three credits were recognized as elective credits.</p><p>5. For those graduate students who shall complete Academic Research Ethics Education Course before the end of their first academic semester, they must follow the regulations of Yuan Ze University Academic Research Ethics Education Course Implementation Highlights. The latest deadline for them shall be their course completions and then their applications towards the degree’s oral exam.</p></td></tr></table>

A minimum of 30 credits are required for graduation, in addition to a master’s thesis. Master students should select their thesis topic at least two weeks before their first year of study.</p><p>2. This degree program’s course requirements include:</p><ol><li> Compulsory courses: 12 credits</li><li> Elective courses: 18 credits (this department requires at least 9 elective credits)</li></ol><p>3. Regular students’ elective courses will not be credited toward vocational course requirements.</p><p>4. If the investigation and qualitative research were repaired, of which three credits for compulsory credits, the other three credits were recognized as elective credits.</p><p>5. For those graduate students who shall complete Academic Research Ethics Education Course before the end of their first academic semester, they must follow the regulations of Yuan Ze University Academic Research Ethics Education Course Implementation Highlights. The latest deadline for them shall be their course completions and then their applications towards the degree’s oral exam.</p></td></tr></table>

A minimum of 30 credits are required for graduation, in addition to a master’s thesis. Master students should select their thesis topic at least two weeks before their first year of study.</p><p>2. This degree program’s course requirements include:</p><ol><li> Compulsory courses: 12 credits</li><li> Elective courses: 18 credits (this department requires at least 9 elective credits)</li></ol><p>3. Regular students’ elective courses will not be credited toward vocational course requirements.</p><p>4. If the investigation and qualitative research were repaired, of which three credits for compulsory credits, the other three credits were recognized as elective credits.</p><p>5. For those graduate students who shall complete Academic Research Ethics Education Course before the end of their first academic semester, they must follow the regulations of Yuan Ze University Academic Research Ethics Education Course Implementation Highlights. The latest deadline for them shall be their course completions and then their applications towards the degree’s oral exam.</p><p> </p></td></tr></table>

A minimum of 30 credits are required for graduation, in addition to a master’s thesis. Master students should select their thesis topic at least two weeks before their first year of study.</p><p>2. This degree program’s course requirements include:</p><ol><li> Compulsory courses: 12 credits</li><li> Elective courses: 18 credits (this department requires at least 9 elective credits)</li></ol><p>3. Regular students’ elective courses will not be credited toward vocational course requirements.</p><p>4. If the investigation and qualitative research were repaired, of which three credits for compulsory credits, the other three credits were recognized as elective credits.</p><p>5. According to the regulations of Yuan Ze University Academic Research Ethics Education Course Implementation regulations, ggraduate students shall complete the academic research ethics education course by the end of their first academic semester or at the latest before their oral qualifying exam. Students who fail to complete the course cannot apply for the degree’s oral qualifying exam.</p><p> </p></td></tr></table>

A minimum of 30 credits are required for graduation, in addition to a master’s thesis. Master students should select their thesis topic at least two weeks before their first year of study.</p><p>2. This degree program’s course requirements include:</p><ol><li> Compulsory courses: 12 credits</li><li> Elective courses: 18 credits (this department requires at least 9 elective credits)</li></ol><p>3. Regular students’ elective courses will not be credited toward vocational course requirements.</p><p>4. If the investigation and qualitative research were repaired, of which three credits for compulsory credits, the other three credits were recognized as elective credits.</p><p>5. According to the regulations of Yuan Ze University Academic Research Ethics Education Course Implementation regulations, ggraduate students shall complete the academic research ethics education course by the end of their first academic semester or at the latest before their oral qualifying exam. Students who fail to complete the course cannot apply for the degree’s oral qualifying exam.</p><p> </p></td></tr></table>

Regular students’ elective courses will not be credited toward vocational course requirements.</p><p>4. If the investigation and qualitative research were repaired, of which three credits for compulsory credits, the other three credits were recognized as elective credits.</p><p>5. According to the regulations of Yuan Ze University Academic Research Ethics Education Course Implementation regulations, ggraduate students shall complete the academic research ethics education course by the end of their first academic semester or at the latest before their oral qualifying exam. Students who fail to complete the course cannot apply for the degree’s oral qualifying exam.</p></td></tr></table>

This degree program’s course requirements include:</p><ol><li> Compulsory courses: 9 credits</li><li> Elective courses: 15 credits (this department requires at least 9 elective credits)</li></ol><p>3. Regular students’ elective courses will not be credited toward vocational course requirements.</p><p>4. If the investigation and qualitative research were repaired, of which three credits for compulsory credits, the other three credits were recognized as elective credits.</p><p>5. For those graduate students who shall complete Academic Research Ethics Education Course before the end of their first academic semester, they must follow the regulations of Yuan Ze University Academic Research Ethics Education Course Implementation Highlights. The latest deadline for them shall be their course completions and then their applications towards the degree’s oral exam.</p></td></tr></table>

**元智大學社會暨政策科學系  碩士在職專班**

YZU Social and Policy Sciences Master Program (Part-time)

**必修科目表** Compulsory Course Chart

**（107學年度入學新生適用）** for students enrolling at the Academic Year 2018

107.05.02 一○六學年度第五次教務會議通過

<table><tr><td rowspan="2"><p>學年</p><p>學期</p><p>科目</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>第一學年First academic year</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>第二學年Second academic year</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>上Fall Semester</p></td><td><p>下Spring Semester</p></td><td><p>上Fall Semester</p></td><td><p>下Spring Semester</p></td></tr><tr><td rowspan="3"><p>必修  </p><p>科目 </p><p>Year of Study,</p><p>Semester</p><p>Subject</p><p>（9）</p></td><td rowspan="2"><p>社會學專題</p><p>Selected Topics in Sociology</p><p>（3）</p><p>SC523</p></td><td><p>調查研究</p><p>Survey Research</p><p>（3）</p><p>SC516</p></td><td rowspan="2"></td><td rowspan="2"></td></tr><tr><td><p>質性研究</p><p>Qualitative Research</p><p>（3）</p><p>SC515</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>論文寫作與指導</p><p>Introduction to</p><p>Thesis Writing</p><p>（3）</p><p>SC522</p></td><td></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td><p>學期學分小計total</p></td><td><p>6</p></td><td><p>3</p></td><td><p>0</p></td><td><p>0</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>備註 </p><p>Remarks</p></td><td colspan="4"><p>1.最低畢業計 24 學分，另加碩士論文一篇。(研究生應於第一學年結束前兩週內選定碩士論文指導教授)</p><p>2.本學程修習之科目包括：</p><ol><li>必修科目：共9學分。（調查研究與質性研究為二選一必修）</li><li>選修科目：共15學分。（本所至少選修9學分）</li></ol><p>3.若調查研究與質性研究均修者，其中三學分為必修學分，另三學分得認列為選修學分。</p><p>4.入學研究生須依本校學術研究倫理教育課程實施要點規定，於入學第一學期結束前完成學術研究倫理教育課程，最遲須於申請學位口試前補修完成，未完成本課程，不得申請學位口試。</p><p>1. A minimum of 24 credits are required for graduation, in addition to a master’s thesis. Master students should select their thesis topic at least two weeks before their first year of study.</p><p>2. This degree program’s course requirements include:</p><ol><li> Compulsory courses: 9 credits</li><li> Elective courses: 15 credits (this department requires at least 9 elective credits)</li></ol><p>3. Regular students’ elective courses will not be credited toward vocational course requirements.</p><p>4. If the investigation and qualitative research were repaired, of which three credits for compulsory credits, the other three credits were recognized as elective credits.</p><p>5. For those graduate students who shall complete Academic Research Ethics Education Course before the end of their first academic semester, they must follow the regulations of Yuan Ze University Academic Research Ethics Education Course Implementation Highlights. The latest deadline for them shall be their course completions and then their applications towards the degree’s oral exam.</p></td></tr></table>

A minimum of 24 credits are required for graduation, in addition to a master’s thesis. Master students should select their thesis topic at least two weeks before their first year of study.</p><p>2. This degree program’s course requirements include:</p><ol><li> Compulsory courses: 9 credits</li><li> Elective courses: 15 credits (this department requires at least 9 elective credits)</li></ol><p>3. Regular students’ elective courses will not be credited toward vocational course requirements.</p><p>4. If the investigation and qualitative research were repaired, of which three credits for compulsory credits, the other three credits were recognized as elective credits.</p><p>5. For those graduate students who shall complete Academic Research Ethics Education Course before the end of their first academic semester, they must follow the regulations of Yuan Ze University Academic Research Ethics Education Course Implementation Highlights. The latest deadline for them shall be their course completions and then their applications towards the degree’s oral exam.</p></td></tr></table>

A minimum of 24 credits are required for graduation, in addition to a master’s thesis. Master students should select their thesis topic at least two weeks before their first year of study.</p><p>2. This degree program’s course requirements include:</p><ol><li> Compulsory courses: 9 credits</li><li> Elective courses: 15 credits (this department requires at least 9 elective credits)</li></ol><p>3. If the investigation and qualitative research were repaired, of which three credits for compulsory credits, the other three credits were recognized as elective credits.</p><p>4. According to the regulations of Yuan Ze University Academic Research Ethics Education Course Implementation regulations, ggraduate students shall complete the academic research ethics education course by the end of their first academic semester or at the latest before their oral qualifying exam. Students who fail to complete the course cannot apply for the degree’s oral qualifying exam.</p></td></tr></table>

A minimum of 24 credits are required for graduation, in addition to a master’s thesis. Master students should select their thesis topic at least two weeks before their first year of study.</p><p>2. This degree program’s course requirements include:</p><ol><li> Compulsory courses: 9 credits</li><li> Elective courses: 15 credits (this department requires at least 9 elective credits)</li></ol><p>3. If the investigation and qualitative research were repaired, of which three credits for compulsory credits, the other three credits were recognized as elective credits.</p><p>4. According to the regulations of Yuan Ze University Academic Research Ethics Education Course Implementation regulations, graduate students shall complete the academic research ethics education course by the end of their first academic semester or at the latest before their oral qualifying exam. Students who fail to complete the course cannot apply for the degree’s oral qualifying exam.</p><p>5. Students who would like to apply for Cross-System Courses need to fill in the "Application for Cross-System Courses" form. Credits taken across academic systems are allowed to be counted as graduation credits, up to a maximum of 6 credits.</p></td></tr></table>

**元智大學社會暨政策科學系  碩士在職專班**

YZU Social and Policy Sciences Master Program (Part-time)

**必修科目表** Compulsory Course Chart

**（113學年度入學新生適用）** for students enrolling at the Academic Year 2024

113.05.01 一一二學年度第八次教務會議通過

113.06.05 一一二學年度第九次教務會議修訂通過

<table><tr><td rowspan="2"><p>學年</p><p>學期</p><p>科目</p></td><td colspan="3"><p>第一學年First academic year</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>第二學年Second academic year</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>上Fall Semester</p></td><td><p>下Spring Semester</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>上Fall Semester</p></td><td><p>下Spring Semester</p></td></tr><tr><td rowspan="2"><p>必修  </p><p>科目 </p><p>Year of Study,</p><p>Semester</p><p>Subject</p><p>（9）</p></td><td><p>SC516</p><p>調查研究</p><p>Survey Research</p><p>（3）</p></td><td rowspan="2"><p>SC522</p><p>論文寫作與指導</p><p>Introduction to</p><p>Thesis Writing</p><p>（3）</p></td><td colspan="2" rowspan="2"></td><td rowspan="2"></td></tr><tr><td><p>SC515</p><p>質性研究</p><p>Qualitative Research</p><p>（3）</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>學期學分小計total</p></td><td><p>3</p></td><td><p>3</p></td><td colspan="2"></td><td><p>0</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>備註 </p><p>Remarks</p></td><td colspan="5"><p>1.最低畢業計 24 學分，另加碩士論文一篇。(研究生應於第一學年結束前兩週內選定碩士論文指導教授)</p><p>2.本學程修習之科目包括：</p><ol><li>必修科目：共6學分。（調查研究與質性研究為二選一必修）</li><li>選修科目：共18學分。（本所至少選修12學分）</li></ol><p>3.若調查研究與質性研究均修者，其中三學分為必修學分，另三學分得認列為選修學分。</p><p>4.研究生須依本校學術研究倫理教育課程實施要點規定，於入學第一學期結束前完成學術研究倫理教育課程。未完成者，最遲須於申請學位口試前補修完成，未完成本課程，不得申請學位口試。</p><p>5.欲跨學制修課之學生，須填寫「元智大學課程跨學制申請表」，跨學制修課之</p><p>  學分數准予納入畢業學分，至多6學分。</p><p>1. A minimum of 24 credits are required for graduation, in addition to a master’s thesis. Master students should select their thesis topic at least two weeks before their first year of study.</p><p>2. This degree program’s course requirements include:</p><ol><li> Compulsory courses: 9 credits</li><li> Elective courses: 15 credits (this department requires at least 9 elective credits)</li></ol><p>3. If the investigation and qualitative research were repaired, of which three credits for compulsory credits, the other three credits were recognized as elective credits.</p><p>4. According to the regulations of Yuan Ze University Academic Research Ethics Education Course Implementation regulations, graduate students shall complete the academic research ethics education course by the end of their first academic semester or at the latest before their oral qualifying exam. Students who fail to complete the course cannot apply for the degree’s oral qualifying exam.</p><p>5. Students who would like to apply for Cross-System Courses need to fill in the "Application for Cross-System Courses" form. Credits taken across academic systems are allowed to be counted as graduation credits, up to a maximum of 6 credits.</p><p> </p></td></tr></table>

**元智大學社會暨政策科學系  碩士在職專班**

**必修科目表 （115學年度入學新生適用）**

**Department of Social and Policy Sciences, Yuan Ze University**

**Master Program (Part-time) Compulsory Course Chart**

**(Applicable to Students Admitted in Academic Year of 2026)**

115.04.29 一一四學年度第七次教務會議通過

Passed by the 7th Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2025, on April 29, 2026

<table><tr><td rowspan="2"><p>學年</p><p>Academic Year</p><p>學期</p><p>Semester</p><p>科目</p><p>Course</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>第一學年</p><p>1<sup>st</sup> Academic Year</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>第二學年</p><p>2<sup>nd</sup> Academic Year</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>上Fall</p></td><td><p>下Spring</p></td><td><p>上Fall</p></td><td><p>下Spring</p></td></tr><tr><td rowspan="2"><p>必修科目</p><p>Required Course</p></td><td><p>SC516</p><p>調查研究</p><p>Survey Research</p><p>（3）</p></td><td><p>SC522</p><p>論文寫作與指導</p><p>Introduction to</p><p>Thesis Writing</p><p>（3）</p></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td><p>SC515</p><p>質性研究</p><p>Qualitative Research</p><p>（3）</p></td><td></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td><p>學期學分小計Credits Each Semester</p></td><td><p>3</p></td><td><p>3</p></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td><p>備註</p><p>Remarks</p></td><td colspan="4"><p>1.最低畢業計 24 學分，另加碩士論文一篇。(研究生應於第一學年結束前兩週內選定碩士論文指導教授)</p><p>2.本學程修習之科目包括：</p><ol><li>必修科目：共6學分。（調查研究與質性研究為二選一必修）</li><li>選修科目：共18學分。（本所至少選修12學分）</li></ol><p>3.若調查研究與質性研究均修者，其中三學分為必修學分，另三學分得認列為選修學分。</p><p>4.研究生須依本校學術研究倫理教育課程實施要點規定，於入學第一學期結束前完成學術研究倫理教育課程。未完成者，最遲須於申請學位口試前補修完成，未完成本課程，不得申請學位口試。</p><p>5.欲跨學制修課之學生，須填寫「元智大學課程跨學制申請表」，跨學制修課之</p><p>  學分數准予納入畢業學分，至多6學分。</p><p>1. A minimum of 24 credits are required for graduation, in addition to a master’s thesis. Master students should select their thesis topic at least two weeks before their first year of study.</p><p>2. This degree program’s course requirements include:</p><ol><li> Compulsory courses: 6 credits</li><li> Elective courses: 18 credits (this department requires at least 12 elective credits)</li></ol><p>3. If the investigation and qualitative research were repaired, of which three credits for compulsory credits, the other three credits were recognized as elective credits.</p><p>4. According to the regulations of Yuan Ze University Academic Research Ethics Education Course Implementation regulations, graduate students shall complete the academic research ethics education course by the end of their first academic semester or at the latest before their oral qualifying exam. Students who fail to complete the course cannot apply for the degree’s oral qualifying exam.</p><p>5. Students who would like to apply for Cross-System Courses need to fill in the "Application for Cross-System Courses" form. Credits taken across academic systems are allowed to be counted as graduation credits, up to a maximum of 6 credits.</p></td></tr></table>
